<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADVANTEST CORPORATION</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></div></div></div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Notes to&#160;Consolidated Financial Statements (Unaudited)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(1)&#160;&#160;Accounting Principles, Procedures and the Presentation of the Consolidated Financial Statements</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)&#160;&#160;Terminology, Form and Method of Preparation of the Consolidated Financial Statements</font></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>Advantest Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) and its consolidated subsidiaries (collectively &#8220;Advantest&#8221;) prepares the consolidated financial statements in accordance with the accounting principles, procedures, terminology, form and method of preparation required
in the United States of America in connection with its issuance of American Depository Shares as established under Accounting Research Bulletins (&#8220;ARB&#8221;), Accounting Principles Board (&#8220;APB&#8221;) statements, Statements of Financial Accounting Standards (&#8220;SFAS&#8221;) and other relevant sources (collectively &#8220;U.S. GAAP&#8221;).</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>Advantest prepared the interim consolidated financial statements that accompany these notes in conformity with U.S. GAAP, consistent in all material respects with those applied in Advantest&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 20-F for the year ended March 31, 2009 except for changes
discussed in Note (2)-(b).</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The interim financial statements are unaudited, but reflect all normal adjustments that are, in the opinion of management, necessary to provide a fair presentation of results for the interim periods presented.&#160;&#160;This interim information should be read with the consolidated
financial statements in Advantest&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 20-F for the year ended March 31, 2009.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Subsequent events have been evaluated through July 31, 2009, which is the date the accompanying consolidated financial statements were issued.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b)&#160;&#160;Preparation of the Consolidated Financial Statements and Registration with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</font></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The Company became listed on the New York Stock Exchange on September 17, 2001 (local time) by means of an issuance of American Depository Shares, and has been filing a Form 20-F (equivalent to the Annual Securities Report in Japan) with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission
since the year ended March 31, 2002.&#160;&#160;Advantest prepares the consolidated financial statements in its Form 20-F in accordance with U.S. GAAP.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(c)&#160;&#160;Significant differences from the preparation of financial statements under Japanese GAAP</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Of the accounting principles, procedures and method of presentation adopted by Advantest, the following is a brief summary description of the significant differences from the preparation of financial statements using the accounting principles, procedure and method of presentation under Japanese GAAP, as required
under the Financial Instruments and Exchange Law of Japan:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(i)&#160; Allowance for compensated absences</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 14.25pt"></font>In accordance with SFAS No. 43, &#8220;Accounting for Compensated Absences&#8221;, an allowance is provided for the right of employees to receive compensated absences in the future.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(ii)&#160; Accrued pension and severance costs</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 29.45pt"></font>In accordance with SFAS No. 87, &#8220;Employers&#8217; Accounting for Pensions&#8221; and SFAS No. 158, &#8220;Employers&#8217; Accounting for Defined Benefit Pension and Other Postretirement Plans&#8221;, the funded status (i.e., the difference between the fair
value of plan assets and the projected benefit obligation) of pension plans is recognized in the consolidated balance sheets.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(iii)&#160; Goodwill</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 29.45pt"></font>In accordance with SFAS No. 142, &#8220;Goodwill and Other Intangible Assets&#8221;, goodwill is no </font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">&#160;</div></div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">- 5 -</font></div>
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2"></div></div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">&#160;</div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADVANTEST CORPORATION</font>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></div></div></div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: normal">Notes to&#160;Consolidated Financial Statements (Unaudited)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div></div></font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div></div></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">longer amortized, but instead is tested for impairment at least annually.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(2) Description of Business and Summary of Significant Accounting Policies and Practices</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25;">
<td style="WIDTH: 27.2pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div></td>
<td style="WIDTH: 27pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(a)</font></div></td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Description of Business</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest manufactures and sells semiconductor and component test system products and mechatronics-related products such as test handlers and device interfaces.&#160;&#160;Advantest also engages in research and development activities and provides maintenance and support services associated with these products.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Description of the business by segment is as follows:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The semiconductor and component test system segment provides customers with test system products for the semiconductor industry and the electronic parts industry.&#160;&#160;Product lines provided in the semiconductor and component test system segment include test systems for memory semiconductors for memory semiconductor
devices and test systems for SoC (&#8220;System-on-a-Chip&#8221;) semiconductors for non memory semiconductor devices.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The mechatronics system segment provides product lines such as test handlers, mechatronic-applied products for handling semiconductor devices, device interfaces that serve as interfaces with the devices that are measured and operations related to nano-technology products.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The services, support and others segment consists of comprehensive customer solutions provided in connection with the above segments, support services, equipment lease business and others.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top" style="LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25;">
<td style="WIDTH: 27.2pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div></td>
<td style="WIDTH: 27pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(b)</font></div></td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Accounting Change and Accounting Standards Not Yet Adopted</font></div></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In December 2007, the FASB issued SFAS No. 141 (revised 2007), &#8220;Business Combinations&#8221; (&#8220;SFAS 141R&#8221;). SFAS 141R establishes principles and requirements for how an acquirer recognizes and measures in its financial statements the identifiable assets acquired, the liabilities assumed, any noncontrolling
interest in the acquiree and the goodwill acquired. SFAS 141R also establishes disclosure requirements to enable the evaluation of the nature and financial effects of the business combination. SFAS 141R is effective for fiscal years beginning on or after December 15, 2008. Advantest adopted SFAS 141R in the first quarter beginning April 1, 2009, which did not have an impact on its consolidated results of operations and financial condition.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In December 2007, the FASB issued SFAS No. 160, &#8220;Noncontrolling Interests in Consolidated Financial Statement, an amendment of ARB No. 51&#8221; (&#8220;SFAS 160&#8221;). SFAS 160 establishes accounting and reporting standards for ownership interests in subsidiaries held by parties other than the parent,
the amount of consolidated net income attributable to the parent and to the noncontrolling interest, changes in a parent&#8217;s ownership interest, and the valuation of retained noncontrolling equity investments when a subsidiary is deconsolidated. SFAS 160 also establishes disclosure requirements that clearly identify and distinguish between the&#160;interests of the parent and the interests of the noncontrolling owners. SFAS 160 is effective for fiscal years beginning on or after December 15, 2008.&#160;&#160;Advantest
adopted SFAS 160 in the first quarter beginning April 1, 2009, which did not have an impact on its consolidated results of operations and financial condition.</font></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADVANTEST CORPORATION</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></div></div></div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Notes to&#160;Consolidated Financial Statements (Unaudited)</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 63pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 17pt"></font>In May 2009, the FASB issued SFAS No. 165, &#8220;Subsequent Events&#8221; (&#8220;SFAS 165&#8221;). SFAS 165 establishes general standards of accounting for and disclosure of events that occur after the balance sheet date but before financial statements are issued or
are available to be issued. SFAS165 requires the disclosure of the date through which subsequent events have been evaluated, as well as whether that date is the date the financial statements were issued or the date the financial statements were available to be issued. SFAS 165 is effective for interim periods ending after June 15, 2009. Advantest adopted SFAS 165 in the first quarter beginning April 1, 2009, which did not have an impact on its financial statements.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div>

<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Reclassification</font></div></td></tr></table></div>

<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">&#160;</div></div>
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">- 8 -</font></div>
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2"></div></div>
<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">&#160;</div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<br>&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADVANTEST CORPORATION</font>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></div></div></div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Notes to&#160;Consolidated Financial Statements (Unaudited)</div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest maintains non-marketable investment securities, which are recorded at cost.&#160;&#160;The carrying amounts of non-marketable investment securities were &#165;3,646 million and &#165;3,664 million at June 30, 2009 and March 31, 2009, respectively. For non-marketable equity securities which Advantest identified events or
changes in circumstances that might have had significant adverse effect on the fair value of the investments, the fair value approximate the carrying value. Advantest has not estimated the fair value of other non-marketable equity securities of &#165;1,726 million and &#165;1,150 million at June 30, 2009 and March 31, 2009, respectively, since it is not practicable to estimate the fair value of the investments. It is because of the lack of readily determinable fair values and difficulty in estimating fair value
without incurring excessive cost.</font></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(5) Derivative Financial Instruments</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Derivative</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest uses foreign exchange forward contracts and currency options to manage currency exposure, resulting from changes in foreign currency exchange rates, on trade receivables.&#160;&#160;However, these contracts do not qualify for hedge accounting since they do not meet the hedging criteria specified by Statement
of Financial Accounting Standards (&#8220;SFAS&#8221;) No. 133, &#8220;Accounting for Derivative Instruments and Hedging Activities&#8221;, as amended.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Foreign exchange contracts generally have maturities of several months.&#160;&#160;These contracts are used to reduce Advantest&#8217;s risk associated with exchange rate movements, as gains and losses on these contracts are intended to offset exchange losses and gains on underlying exposures.&#160;&#160;Changes in fair
value of foreign exchange contracts are recognized in earnings under the caption of other income (expense).</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest does not, as a matter of policy, enter into derivative transactions for the purpose of speculation.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest had foreign exchange contracts to exchange currencies among Japanese yen, US dollar and Euro at June 30, 2009 and March 31 2009. The notional amounts of these contracts at June 30, 2009 and March 31, 2009 were as follows:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">

<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Concentration of credit risk</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Derivative financial instruments contain an element of risk in the event the counterparties are unable to meet the terms of the agreements.&#160;&#160;However, Advantest minimizes risk exposure by limiting the counterparties to major international banks and financial institutions meeting established credit guidelines.&#160;&#160;Management
of Advantest does not expect any counterparty to default on its obligations and, therefore, does not expect to incur any losses due to counterparty default on its obligations.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest generally does not require or place collateral for these derivative financial instruments.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 27.5pt"></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Disclosure about the fair value of Financial Instruments</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The following table presents the carrying amounts and estimated fair values of Advantest&#8217;s financial instruments at&#160;June 30, 2009 and March 31, 2009, except for cash and cash equivalents, short-term investments, trade receivables, other current assets, trade accounts payable and accrued expenses for which
fair value approximate their carrying amounts.&#160;&#160;Fair value estimates are made at a specific point in time based on relevant market information and information about the financial instrument.&#160;&#160;These estimates are subjective in nature and involve uncertainties and matters of significant judgment and, therefore, cannot be determined with precision.&#160;&#160;Changes in assumptions could significantly affect the estimates.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The carrying amounts shown in the table are included in the consolidated balance sheets under the indicated captions.&#160;&#160;And the carrying amounts of foreign exchange contracts are included in other current assets and other current liabilities.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The following methods and assumptions were used to estimate the fair value of each class of financial instruments:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Cash and cash equivalents, short-term investments, trade receivables, other current assets, trade accounts payable, and accrued expenses (nonderivatives)</font>:&#160;&#160;The carrying amounts approximate fair value because of the short maturity of these instruments.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Available-for-sale equity securities</font>:&#160;&#160;The fair values of available-for-sale equity securities are based on quoted market prices at the reporting date for those investments.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Foreign exchange contracts</font>:&#160;&#160;The fair value of foreign exchange contracts are estimated by obtaining quotes from financial institutions.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right">&#160;</div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ADVANTEST CORPORATION</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="left">
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div>
<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></div></div></div></div></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">Notes to&#160;Consolidated Financial Statements (Unaudited)</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 27.5pt"></font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Fair Value Hierarchy</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 15pt"></font>SFAS 157 establishes a fair value hierarchy that prioritizes the inputs to valuation techniques used to measure fair value into the following three levels:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Level 1</font> - Quoted prices (unadjusted) in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that the reporting entity has the ability to access at the measurement date.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Level 2</font> - Observable inputs other than quoted prices included within Level 1 for the asset or liability, either directly or indirectly.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic">Level 3</font> - Unobservable inputs for the asset or liability.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Assets/Liabilities Measured at Fair Value on a Recurring Basis</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 45pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As of June 30, 2009 and as of March 31, 2009, carrying amount of financial assets and liabilities that were measured at fair value on a recurring basis by level is as follows:</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt" align="left">

<td valign="bottom" width="14%" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 4px double; TEXT-ALIGN: right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline">-</font></font></td>
<td nowrap valign="bottom" width="1%" style="PADDING-BOTTOM: 4px; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td></tr></table></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The table does not include assets and liabilities which are measured at historical cost or any basis other than fair value. Advantest&#8217;s financial assets and liabilities measured at fair value consist of available-for-sale equity securities and foreign exchange contracts. Adjustments to fair value of available-for-sale
equity securities are recorded as an increase or decrease, net of tax, in accumulated other comprehensive income (loss) except where losses are considered to be other than temporary, in which case the losses are recorded in other income (expense). Changes in fair value of foreign exchange contracts are recognized in earnings under the caption of other income (expense).</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(7) Income Taxes</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 15pt"></font>As of June 30, 2008, the estimated annual effective tax rate for FY2008 is approximately 59.4 percent. The estimated annual effective tax rate for FY2008 differs from the 40.4 percent statutory income tax rate primarily due to the effects of foreign tax rates and
undistributed earnings of foreign subsidiaries.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 15pt"></font>As of June 30, 2009, the estimated annual effective tax rate for FY2009 is approximately (0.2) percent. The estimated annual effective tax rate for FY2009 differs from the 40.4 percent statutory income tax rate primarily due to the estimated net increase in valuation allowance
for deferred tax assets and the effects of foreign tax rates.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(9)&#160;&#160;Stock-Based Compensation</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In April 2009, stock options were issued to certain employees of foreign subsidiaries under a stock option plan approved by the Board of Directors.&#160;&#160;The number of granted shares totaled 12,000.&#160;&#160;Options were granted with an exercise price of &#165;2,653 per share that is equal to the higher
of (1) 1.05 times the average price of the Company&#8217;s common shares of the preceding month on the date of grant, (2) the closing price of the Company&#8217;s common shares traded on the Tokyo Stock Exchange on the date of grant and (3) &#165;2,653 per share that is equal to the exercise price of the July 2008 options.&#160;&#160;The options have an exercise period of 4 years and are exercisable from May 1, 2009.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Stock based compensation expense recognized was &#165;2 million, which was included in selling, general and administrative expenses for the three months ended June 30, 2009. No tax benefit was recognized for the three months ended June 30, 2009.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The weighted average fair value per share for stock option that was granted during the three months ended June 30, 2009 was &#165;189.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">(Operating Segment Information)</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 27pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 1.25; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Advantest manufactures and sells semiconductor and component test system products and mechatronics-related products such as test handlers and device interfaces. Advantest also engages in research and development activities and provides maintenance and support services associated with these products. In accordance
with SFAS No. 131, &#8220;Disclosure about Segments of an Enterprise and Related Information&#8221;, Advantest has three operating and reportable segments, which are the design, manufacturing, and sale of semiconductor and component test systems, mechatronics systems and services, support and others. These operating segments are determined based on the nature of the products and the markets.</font></div>
